i < n_leading_bits; ++i) {\n    bucket = (bucket << 1) | binary[63 - i];\n  }\n\n  // Count leading zeros in remaining bits\n  uint64_t leading_zeros = 0;\n  for (uint64_t i = 0; i < 64 - n_leading_bits; The real problem though is that GetOverflowBucketofIndex uses operator[] on the map, which creates default entries, but GetDenseBucket() accesses dense_bucket_[0] directly. But in PrestoCase2, n_leading_bits = 0, which satisfies that condition, so the constructor exits before setting up the dense_bucket_. That's the bug—I need to change the guard condition to n_leading_bits < 0 instead, so that n_leading_bits = 0 still initializes the necessary data i < n_bits_; ++i) {\n    bucket = (bucket << 1) | ((hash >> (BITSET_CAPACITY - 1 - i)) & 1ULL);\n  }\n\n  // Count leading zeros in remaining bits\n  // Find the position of the first 1 bit in the remaining bits (bits 0 to BITSET_CAPACITY - n_bits_ - 1)\n  uint64_t position = 0;\n  int64_t remaining_bits = BITSET_CAPACITY - n_bits_;\n\n  for (int64_t i = remaining_bits - 1; i < m; ++i) {\n      sum += std::pow(2.0, -static_cast<double>(registers_[i]));\n    }\n  }\n\n  double result = CONSTANT * m * m / sum;\n  cardinality_ = static_cast<size_t>(result);\n}\n\ntemplate class HyperLogLog<int64_t>;\ntemplate class HyperLogLog<std::string>;\n\n}  // namespace bustub\n","structuredPatch":[{"oldStart":78,"oldLines":7,"newStart":78,"newLines":7,"lines":[" "," template <typename KeyType>"," auto HyperLogLog<KeyType>::ComputeCardinality() -> void {","-  if (n_bits_ <= 0) {","+  if (n_bits_ < 0) {","     cardinality_ = 0;","     return;","   }"]}],"userModified":false,"replaceAll":false}}

If position = 21, the math works out correctly.\n\nSo the position equals the highest bit index plus one. For hash value 1, bit 20 is the highest set bit, making position = 21.
